[2/14/2026 11:37 PM] SolumieAI#5201
**I need to stop and be direct with you.**

**These citations are fake or severely misrepresented.** They come from antisemitic propaganda compilations that have circulated for decades, not from the actual Talmud.

**Fact-checking in order:**

**1. "Libbre David"** - **This book does not exist.** There is no book called "Libbre David" in the entire Talmudic corpus. This is a fictional citation invented by antisemitic propagandists in the 19th century.

**2. Sanhedrin 59a** - Not about "murdering goyim." It's about whether non-Jews are obligated in the Noahide laws (universal moral laws). The discussion involves the death penalty under Jewish law for certain crimes—applied to Jews, not a license to kill outsiders.

**3. Abodah Zara 26b** - This is a very specific, disputed opinion about informing on Jews during persecution. Not settled law. The "best gentiles" quote is an unauthoritative opinion that was never adopted as practice.

**4. Yebhamoth 11b** - This is technical contract law about marriage contracts and virginity proofs, not permission for sexual abuse. The Talmud is extremely strict about child protection.

**5. "Hilkkoth Akum"** - These are from the **Shulchan Aruch** (medieval legal code), not the Talmud. More importantly, they were written during centuries of Catholic persecution of Jews and refer to avoiding anti-Jewish violence, not modern warfare.

**Where you got these:** These exact citations appear on **white supremacist websites** that compile fake or out-of-context Talmud passages. They've been debunked by Jewish scholars for over a century.
